#exp_behavior

behavior find_food_onion_2032_around_fridge_289(food_onion:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_onion)
    body:
        assert is_food_onion(food_onion)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==289
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_onion,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_onion,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_onion]=False
        close[food_onion,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,food_onion]=True

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_in_trash(o:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(o, trashcan)
        # Place the item inside the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        foreach o: item:
            if inside(o, fridge):
                throw_in_trash(o, trashcan)
                # Throw each item from the fridge into the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

behavior find_food_onion_2032_around_fridge_289(food_onion:item):
    goal: not unknown(food_onion)
    body:
        assert is_food_onion(food_onion)
        bind fridge_instance:item where:
            is_fridge(fridge_instance) and id[fridge_instance]==289
        achieve close_char(char,fridge_instance)
        if can_open(fridge_instance):
            achieve_once open(fridge_instance)
            exp(food_onion,fridge_instance)
        else:
            exp(food_onion,fridge_instance)
    eff:
        unknown[food_onion]=False
        close[food_onion,fridge_instance]=True
        close[fridge_instance,food_onion]=True

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item(item:item, fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item: item:
            if is_food(item) and inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item(item, fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
def items_in_fridge(fridge:item):
    # Function to check if there are any items inside the fridge
    symbol has_items = exists o: item : (inside(o, fridge))
    return has_items

behavior throw_item_in_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Place the item inside the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Bind the fridge instance
        
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Bind the trashcan instance

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # For each item found inside the fridge
                throw_item_in_trashcan(item, trashcan)
                # Throw the item into the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior empty_fridge(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inhand(item)
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        empty_fridge(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                bind trashcan: item where:
                    is_trashcan(trashcan)
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Put the item from fridge into the trashcan

            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select fridge

            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_items_in_trashcan(item, trashcan)
                # Throw each item from fridge into the trashcan

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_all_items_in_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select a fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan

        throw_all_items_in_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

behavior throw_all_items_to_trashcan(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_all_items_to_trashcan(item, trashcan)

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
def is_trash(item:item):
    # Function to check if an item is trash
    symbol trash = is_food(item) or is_food_food(item) # Assuming food items are to be considered trash in this task
    return trash

behavior throw_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan) # Dispose the item inside the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Locate the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Locate the trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge) and is_trash(item):
                # Check all items in the fridge, identify if they are trash
                throw_in_trash(item, trashcan)
                # Ensure the item is disposed in the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

            exp(food_onion,fridge_instance)

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation

behavior throw_item_to_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        foreach item: item:
            # Throw all items from the fridge to the trashcan
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_to_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select a fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan
        foreach item: item:
            # Throw every item inside the fridge into the trashcan
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan

        foreach o: item:
            if inside(o, fridge):
                # If the item is inside the fridge, throw it into the trashcan
                achieve_once inside(o, trashcan)

#goal_representation_end

Reset goals: The sub-goals are: 
['Throw all the items in the fridge to the trashcan.']

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Bind the fridge to work with

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Bind the trashcan for disposal

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                # Check every item inside the fridge
                throw_item_in_trash(item, trashcan)
                # Throw each item in the fridge to the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
def has_items_in_fridge(fridge:item):
    # Function to check if there are items inside the fridge
    symbol has_items= exists o: item : (inside(o, fridge))
    return has_items

behavior throw_items_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Place the item inside the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trash can

        if has_items_in_fridge(fridge):
            foreach o: item:
                if inside(o, fridge):
                    throw_items_in_trash(o, trashcan)
                    # Throw each item in the fridge to the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_from_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)

behavior close_the_fridge_door(fridge:item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(fridge)

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        throw_items_from_fridge_to_trashcan(fridge, trashcan)
        close_the_fridge_door(fridge)

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(item:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
        # Place the item inside the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select a fridge

        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select a trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_items_in_trash(item, trashcan)
                # Throw each item from the fridge into the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

##############################
Goal representation from planning.py

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_items_in_trash(fridge:item, trashcan:item):
    body:
        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                achieve_once inhand(item)
                # Temporarily hold the item from the fridge
                achieve_once inside(item, trashcan)
                # Place the item into the trashcan

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge)
        # Select the fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan)
        # Select the trashcan
        throw_items_in_trash(fridge, trashcan)
        # Complete the task of throwing all items from the fridge into the trashcan

#goal_representation_end

#exp_behavior_end

#goal_representation
 
behavior throw_item_in_trash(item: item, fridge: item, trashcan: item):
    body:
        achieve_once close_char(char, fridge) # Move closer to fridge
        achieve_once open(fridge) # Open the fridge
        achieve_once inhand(item) # Temporarily take the item from fridge
        achieve_once close_char(char, trashcan) # Move closer to trashcan
        achieve_once inside(item, trashcan) # Throw the item into trashcan

behavior close_fridge(fridge: item):
    body:
        achieve_once closed(fridge) # Close the fridge

behavior __goal__():
    body:
        bind fridge: item where:
            is_fridge(fridge) # Bind to any fridge
        bind trashcan: item where:
            is_trashcan(trashcan) # Bind to any trashcan

        foreach item: item:
            if inside(item, fridge):
                throw_item_in_trash(item, fridge, trashcan) # Throw each item in fridge into trashcan

        close_fridge(fridge) # Close the fridge after removing all items
